                      <hy-heading heading=h3 id=news section=landingsection>
        News
      </hy-heading>
    
          
            <div>
        <div class="hy-entity-list news-listing--container news-listing-id--145767" data-list-id=145767 data-show-filters=0>
        <input type="hidden" id="pid-145767" name="pid" value="145767">

            The Future of Education

    </div>
  </div>
              <div>


  <div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text-paragraph paragraph--view-mode--default">
    
              <hy-main-content-wrapper>
                	          <hy-heading heading=h2 id="the-best-place-to-work" section=landingsection>
            The best place to work
          </hy-heading>
              
      <hy-paragraph-text variant=main_front_page placement=external>
        
            <div><p>One of our strategic choices is to support the wellbeing, inclusivity and equality of our community. In 2030, we want to be the best place to study, teach, research and work. Could the University of Helsinki be a good workplace for you too?</p>
</div>
      
      </hy-paragraph-text>

                    <hy-box mb="1.75, 1.75, 2, 2.5"></hy-box>
      
              </hy-main-content-wrapper>

            Open and multidisciplinary research  for the world
          </hy-heading>
              
      <hy-paragraph-text variant=main_front_page placement=external>
        
            <div><p>Our multidisciplinary research university creates opportunities for cooperation that transcends borders betweentraditional fields of science. Openness strengthens research and its impact on society. Get to know our research, our researchers and the services that we offer to our researchers.</p>

  <div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text-paragraph paragraph--view-mode--default">
    
              <hy-main-content-wrapper>
              
      <hy-paragraph-text variant=main_front_page placement=external>
        
            <div><p>The University of Helsinki is located in Finland. It is the oldest and largest institution of academic education in the country. The university is an international scientific community of 40,000 students and researchers. In international university rankings, the University of Helsinki typically ranks among the top 100. Through the power of science, the University has contributed to society, education and welfare since 1640.</p>
</div>
